#!/bin/sh

work_dir="work_dir"
name_prefix="gl-pt--fasttext"
model_name=${name_prefix}"-model.bin"
decode=${name_prefix}"-result.txt"
mkdir -p ${work_dir}
echo save results to ${work_dir}

#python nmt.py \
#    train \
#    --langs 'gl-en,pt-en'\
#    --lang-embed-size 8\
#    --cuda \
#    --vocab-size 20000 \
#    --save-to ${work_dir}/${model_name} \

#    --max-epoch 100 \
#    --embed-size 200 \
#    --uniform-init 0.1 \

for lang in pt

    ${work_dir}/${model_name} ${lang} en ${work_dir}/decode-${lang}.txt
